Реклама
Реклама
Реклама
Реклама
Реклама
Pokemon
Go:
новая
мобильная
игра
покорила
пользователей
сети
Мобильное
приложение
положительно
влияет
на
здоровье
игроков.
Образ
жизни
11.07.2016
Текст
Тимур
Акулов
Комментарии
Pokemon
Go
–
это
новое
мобильное
приложение
для
iOS
и
Android,
которое,
по
сообщениям
геймеров,
положительно
влияет
на
их
здоровье.
Об
этом
пользователи
сети
сообщили
сами,
написав
в
свои Твиттер-аккаунты.
Геймеры
признались,
что
охота
на
виртуальных
монстров
помогает
им
улучшить
их
психическое
состояние.
Кто-то
отметил,
что
Pokemon
Go
«творит
чудеса»
и
«стимулирует
лишний
раз
выйти
на
улицу».
А
кто-то
рассказал,
что
игрушка
помогает
справиться
с
депрессией
и
тревожными
мыслями.
Кроме
того,
программа
помогает
исследовать
мир,
подстёгивая
выйти
из
дома.
Игроки
по
всему
миру
отмечают,
что
новая
чудо-игрушка
заставляет
их
не
просто
сидеть,
уткнувшись в
телефон,
а
ходить
и
дышать
свежим
воздухом.
Фишка
игры
в
том,
что
на
использует
функции
дополненной
реальности.
Цель
Pokemon
Go
в
том,
чтобы
ходить
по
местности
и
искать
фантастических
зверушек,
драться
с
покемонами
других
участников
в
виртуальных
поединках.
В
игре
нужно
заниматься
исследованием
окружающего
пространства,
чтобы
найти
и
поймать
больше
100
покемонов
разных
видов.
Несмотря
на

у

не

—

.artist_name").html(data.show_title);
					
					var
show_link
=
"/show.php?show_id="+data.show_id;
					if(data.show_sanitized_url
!=
""){
						show_link
=
"/podcasts/"+data.show_sanitized_url;
					}
					$(".track_info_container
.current
.artist_name").attr("href",show_link);
					$(".player_container
.player
.progress_container
.station_logo").attr("src",data.big_thumb_url);
				}
			}
		}
		
		/**
		
*
Recursive
function
that
animates
the
song
name
if
the
content
is
wider
than
the
container
		
*/
		function
animateSongTitle(){
			var
pos
=
$(".player_container
.current
.title_container
.song_title").css("margin-left");
			var
width
=
$(".player_container
.current
.title_container
.song_title").width();
			var
parentWidth
=
$(".player_container
.current
.title_container").width();
			
			var
toSet
=
parseInt(parentWidth)
-
parseInt(width);
			if(parseInt(pos)
<
0){
				toSet
=
0;
			}
			if(toSet
<=
0)
				$(".player_container
.current
.song_title").delay(3000).animate({"margin-left"
:
toSet},(-1*(parseInt(parentWidth)
-
parseInt(width)))*100,function(){animateSongTitle()});
		}
		
		function
convertToMMSS(seconds){
			if(seconds
>
0){
				seconds
=
Number(seconds);
				var
m
=
Math.floor(seconds
/
60);
				var
s
=
Math.floor(seconds
%
60);
				return
((m
<
10
?
"0"
:
"")
+
m
+
":"
+
(s
<
10
?
"0"
:
"")
+
s);

			}
			return
"00:00";
		}

		
		function
togglePlay(){
			if(active_player
==
"radio"
&&
player
==
null){
				if(typeof
active_station
!==
"undefined"
&&
active_station
!=
null)
					selectStation(active_station.id);
				else
					shuffle();
				return;
			}
			else
if(active_player
==
"podcast"
&&
podcast_player
==
null){
				return
false;
			}
			
			if(is_playing){
				if(active_player
==
"radio")
					player.stop();
				else
					podcast_player.pause();
			}
			else{
				if(active_player
==
"radio")
					player.play();
				else{
					if(is_paused)
						podcast_player.resume();
					else
						podcast_player.play();
				}
			}
		}
		
		
		
		function
shuffle(){
			
			if(typeof
active_station
!==
"undefined"
&&
active_station
!=
null){
				shuffle_history.push(active_station.id);
			}
			
			var
keys
=
[];
			$.each(stations,function(index,station){
				keys.push(index);
			});
			
			var
random_station
=
Math.floor(Math.random()
*
keys.length)

;

			while(active_station
!=
null
&&
active_station.id
==
stations[keys[random_station]].id){
				random_station
=
Math.floor(Math.random()
*
keys.length)

;

			}
			var
event_text
=
(active_station
!=
null
?
("from:"
+
active_station.mount
+
"-"
+

active_station.id)
:
"")
+
"to:"
+
stations[keys[random_station]].mount
+
"-"
+
stations[keys[random_station]].id;
			trackEvent("Chameleon
Player","Shuffle",event_text);
			selectStation(stations[keys[random_station]].id,true,false);
		}
		
		function
setPlayerVolume(toSet){
			if(toSet
>
70){
				$(".player
.volume_container").addClass("loud");
			}
			else{
				$(".player
.volume_container").removeClass("loud");
			}
			if(toSet
<
30
&&
toSet
>
0){
				$(".player
.volume_container").addClass("quite");
			}
			else{
				$(".player
.volume_container").removeClass("quite");	
			}
			if(toSet
==
0)
				$(".player
.volume_container").addClass("muted");
			else
				$(".player
.volume_container").removeClass("muted");
	
			if(player
!=
null){
				player.setVolume(toSet);
			}
			if(podcast_player
!=
null)
				podcast_player.setVolume(toSet);
		}
		
		function
toggleMute(){
			if(!$(".volume_container").hasClass("muted")){
				var
value
=
$(".volume_container
.volume_slider").slider("value");
				$(".volume_container").attr("value_before_mute",value);
				$(".volume_container
.volume_slider").slider("value",0);
				setPlayerVolume(0);	
			}
			else{
				var
value
=
$(".volume_container").attr("value_before_mute");
				
				if(isNaN(value))
					value
=
10;
					
				$(".volume_container
.volume_slider").slider("value",value);
				setPlayerVolume(value);	
			}
		}
		
		function
toggleStationList(){
			
			var
windowWidth
=
$(window).width();
			
			if(!$(".station_list_container").hasClass("open")){
				if(windowWidth<480){
					globalBodyScrollTop
=
$("body").scrollTop();
					globalHtmlScrollTop
=
$("html").scrollTop();
					globalMaxScrollTop
=
Math.max(globalBodyScrollTop,globalHtmlScrollTop);
					
					$(".station_list_container").css("top",margin).slideDown(200,function(){$(".station_list_container").addClass("open");});
					$(".blurry_container",$(".station_list_container")).width($(".player_container
.blurry_container").width());
					$(".main").slideUp(200);
					var
margin
=
117;
					if($(".superbar
nav").hasClass("open"))
						margin
=
163;
					$(".selector_toggle").addClass("active");
					tempScrollTop
=
46-$(".superbar").height()
+
1;
					$("body,html").scrollTop(tempScrollTop);
					oldScrollTop
=
globalMaxScrollTop;
				}
				else{
					$(".blurry_container",$(".station_list_container")).width($(".player_container
.blurry_container").width());
					$(".station_list_container").animate({left:0},200,function(){$(".station_list_container").addClass("open");});
					$(".selector_toggle").addClass("active");	
				}
					
				trackEvent("Chameleon
Web","Station
List
Toggle","Open");
			}
			else{
				$(".main").slideDown(200);
				if(windowWidth<480){
					$(".station_list_container").slideUp(200,function(){
						$(".station_list_container").removeClass("open").removeAttr("style");
						$(".selector_toggle").removeClass("active");
						$("body,html").scrollTop(oldScrollTop);
					});
				}
				else
					$(".station_list_container").animate({left:-400},200,function(){$(".station_list_container").removeClass("open");});
					$(".selector_toggle").removeClass("active");
					
				trackEvent("Chameleon
Web","Station
List
Toggle","Close");
			}
		}
		
		
		$(document).ready(function(e)
{
			$(".volume_container
.volume_slider").slider({
				

orientation:
"vertical",
				

range:
"max",
				

min:
0,
				

max:
100,
				

value:
80,
				

slide:
function(
event,
ui
)
{
						var
toSet
=
ui.value;
						setPlayerVolume(toSet);
				

}
			});
			
			if(is_autoplay){
				setTimeout(function(){togglePlay();},5000);
			}
		});
		
		function
updateCurrentSong(){
			$.ajax({
				
url		:
"https://handlers.chameleon.fm/api.functions.php"
				,data
	:
{
					
"command"
:
"get_current_song"
					,"station_id":"all"
				}
				,type:"POST"
				,dataType:"jsonp"
				,success:
function(response){
					
					$.each(stations,function(index,station){
						var
station_element
=
$(".station[station_id="+station.id+"]");
						if(station_element.length
>
0){
							var
id
=
station.id;
							if(typeof(response.data["station_"+id])
!==
"undefined"){
								var
song
=
response.data["station_"+id]["current_song"];
								station["current_song"]
=
song;
								
								$(".song_title",station_element).html(song.title);
								var
artist_name
=
song.artist_name;
								if(song.feat_artist_id
!=
"")
									artist_name
+=
"
feat.
"
+
song.feat_artist_name;
									
								$(".artist_name",station_element).html(artist_name);
								if(typeof
song.url_artist_images_16_9
!==
"undefined"){
									if($(".artist_image.loaded",station_element).attr("src")
!=
song.url_artist_images_16_9[0])
										$(".artist_image.loaded",station_element).attr("src",song.url_artist_images_16_9[0]);
									if($(".artist_image",station_element).not(".loaded").attr("org_src")
!=
song.url_artist_images_16_9[0])
										$(".artist_image",station_element).not(".loaded").attr("org_src",song.url_artist_images_16_9[0]);
								}
								$(station_element).attr("duration",song.duration_sec);
								$(station_element).attr("position",song.position);
							}
						}
					});
					loadImages();
				
}
				,error:
function(){}
			});
		}
		
		function
updateDurations(){
			
			clearTimeout(song_timer);
			if(active_player
==
"radio"){
				song_check_counter
++;
				if(song_check_counter
%
30
==
1)
					updateCurrentSong();
						
				if(active_song
!=
null){
					if(typeof
active_song.time_elapsed
===
"undefined"
||
isNaN(active_song.time_elapsed)){
						active_song.time_elapsed
=
0;
					}
					if(typeof
active_song.duration_sec
===
"undefined"
||
isNaN(active_song.duration_sec)){
						active_song.duration_sec
=
0;
					}
					active_song.duration_sec
=
Number(active_song.duration_sec);
					active_song.time_elapsed++;
		
					if(active_song.time_elapsed
>
active_song.duration_sec)
						active_song.time_elapsed
=
active_song.duration_sec;
						
					$(".active_song_position,
.timeshift_position").text(convertToMMSS(active_song.time_elapsed));
					$(".active_song_duration,
.timeshift_duration").text(convertToMMSS(active_song.duration_sec));
					
					var
progress
=
(active_song.duration_sec)
>
0
?
(100*active_song.time_elapsed/active_song.duration_sec)
:
0;
					$(".player
.progress_container
.bar").width(progress
+
"%");
				}
				
				$(".station").each(function(index,station_element){
					if(typeof
$(station_element).attr("duration")
!==
"undefined"
&&
$(station_element).attr("duration")
!=
null
&&
$(station_element).attr("duration")
!=
""){
						var
duration
=
parseInt($(station_element).attr("duration"));
						var
position
=
parseInt($(station_element).attr("position"));
						position
++;
						if(position
>
duration){
							position
=
duration;
						}
						$(station_element).attr("duration",duration);
						$(station_element).attr("position",position);
						$(".bar",$(station_element)).width(Math.floor(position*100/duration)
+
"%");
					}
				});
				song_timer
=
setTimeout(updateDurations,1000);
			}
			
		}

		var
podcast_player
=
null;
		function
playShowEpisode(to_play){

			if(active_player
==
"podcast"
&&
active_podcast
!=
null
&&
to_play
==
active_podcast.id){
				if(podcast_player.paused)
					podcast_player.resume();
				else
					podcast_player.pause();
					
				return;
			}
			
			$("header
.player_container").addClass("podcast_mode");
			active_player
=
"podcast";
			
			soundManager.stopAll();
			if(player
!=
null)
				player.stop();
			
			$.ajax({
				
url
		:
"https://handlers.chameleon.fm/api.functions.php"
				,dataType	:
"jsonp"
				,type		:
"POST"
				,data	:
{	

					
"command"
:
"get_show_episode"
					,"episode_id":to_play
				}
				,success:
function(response){
					if($.isEmptyObject(response)
||
!response.result
||
$.isEmptyObject(response.data)){
						//TODO,
show
error;
						return
false;
					}
					
					if
((typeof
response.data.media_url
===
"undefined")
||
!soundManager.canPlayURL(response.data.media_url))
{
						//TODO,
show
error;
						return
false;
					}
					
					
					if(podcast_player
!=
null)
						podcast_player.destruct();
					
					var
slider_volume
=
$(".volume_container
.volume_slider").slider("value");
					if(isNaN(slider_volume))
						slider_volume
=
50;
					
					updateSongInfo(response.data);
					podcast_player
=
soundManager.createSound({
						id:
'podcast',
						url:
response.data.media_url,
						volume:slider_volume
					});
					
					$("header
.progress_bar
.loading_bar").width(0);
					
					podcast_player.play({
						
onpause
:
function(){
							set_player_status(false);
							is_paused
=
true;
							$(".player
.action.play
.icon,
.station.station_item.active
.icon").addClass("icon_play").removeClass("icon_stop").removeClass("icon_pause");
						
}
						,onresume
:
function(){
							set_player_status(true);
							is_paused
=
false;
							$(".player
.action.play
.icon,
.station.station_item.active
.icon").removeClass("icon_play").removeClass("icon_stop").addClass("icon_pause");
						
}
						,whileplaying
:
function(){
							set_player_status(true);
							is_paused
=
false;
							$(".player
.action.play
.icon,
.station.station_item.active
.icon").removeClass("icon_play").removeClass("icon_pause").addClass("icon_pause");
							
							var
position
=
convertToMMSS(this.position/1000);
							var
duration
=
convertToMMSS(this.duration/1000);
							$(".active_song_position,
.timeshift_position").text(position);
							$(".active_song_duration,
.timeshift_duration").text(duration);
							
							var
progress
=
(this.position)
>
0
?
(100*this.position/this.duration)
:
0;
							$(".player
.progress_container
.bar").width(progress
+
"%");
						
}
						,whileloading
:
function(){
							if(active_player
!=
"podcast")
								return;
								
							var
widthToSet
=
100*this.bytesLoaded/this.bytesTotal;
							
							if(widthToSet
>
98
)
								widthToSet
=
100;
							
							$("header
.progress_bar
.loading_bar").width(widthToSet
+
"%");
						}
						,onfinish
:
function(){
							set_player_status(false);
							is_paused
=
false;
							$(".player
.action.play
.icon,
.station.station_item.active
.icon").addClass("icon_play").removeClass("icon_pause").removeClass("icon_stop");
							playNext();
						
}
						,onstop
:
function(){
							set_player_status(false);
							is_paused
=
false;
							$(".player
.action.play
.icon,
.station.station_item.active
.icon").addClass("icon_play").removeClass("icon_pause").removeClass("icon_stop");
						
}				
					});
					
				}
			});
		}

				share_url
	
=

("https://chameleon.fm/"+(active_song.sanitized_url

				share_thumb

		function
share(service,
url,
thumb,
title,
desc,
username)
{
			var
pWidth
=
620;
			var
pHeight
=
400;
			var
pURL
=
'';
			if
(service
==
"facebook")
{
				pURL
=
'https://www.facebook.com/sharer/sharer.php?s=100&p[title]='+encodeURIComponent(title)+'&p[url]='+encodeURIComponent(url)+'&p[summary]='+encodeURIComponent(desc)+'&p[images][0]='+encodeURIComponent(thumb);
			}
			else
if
(service
==
"twitter")
{
				pURL
=
'https://twitter.com/share?url='
+
encodeURIComponent(url)
+
'&text='
+
encodeURIComponent(desc)
+
'&via='
+
username;
			}
			else
if
(service
==
"vk")
{
				pURL
=
'https://vk.com/share.php?url='
+
encodeURIComponent(url)
+

'&title='+encodeURIComponent(title)+'&image='+encodeURIComponent(thumb)+'&description='+encodeURIComponent(desc);
			}

			else
if
(service
==
"odnoklassniki")
{
				pURL

=
'https://www.odnoklassniki.ru/dk?st.cmd=addShare&st.s=1&st.s=1'+'&st._surl='



+
encodeURIComponent(url)+'&st.comments='
+
encodeURIComponent(title)
;
			}
			else
{
				
return
false;
			}
			togglePlayerShare();
			window.open(pURL,
'sharewindow',
'height='+pHeight+',
width='+pWidth+',
top='+($(window).height()/2
-
(pHeight/2))
+',
left='+$(window).width()/2
+',
toolbar=0,
location=0,
menubar=0,
directories=0,
scrollbars=0');
		}

		function
onYouTubeIframeAPIReady()
{
			loadYTVideos();

		function
loadYTVideos(){
			var
ytWidth
=
'100%';
			var
ytHeight
=
'350';
			
			if(typeof(isMobile)
!==
"undefined"
&&
isMobile
==
true){
				var
ytWidth
=
'300';
				var
ytHeight
=
'170';
			}
			
			$(".youtube_player").each(function(index,
element)
{
				new
YT.Player($(element).attr("id"),
{
					height:
ytHeight,
					width:
ytWidth,
					videoId:
$(element).attr("youtube-id"),
					playerVars:
{
						wmode:
"transparent"
					},
					events:
{
						'onStateChange':
function(event)
{
							if
(event.data
==
YT.PlayerState.PLAYING)
{
								if(is_playing){
									togglePlay();
								}
							}
						}
					}
				});
			});
		}

		function
showMobileNews(){
			if($(window).width()
<=
768
&&
!$("body").hasClass("channel")){

		function
trackEvent(category,action,label){
			debug("EVENT:"

+
"
-
"

-
"

			_gaq.push(["karnaval._trackEvent",

label]);	
		}
		function
openLink(toOpen,log_history){
			if(typeof(log_history)
===
"undefined")
				log_history
=
true;
				
			
			trackEvent("Chameleon
Web","Click
Link",toOpen);
			
			$.ajax({
				url
:
toOpen
				,dataType:"html"
				,data:{
					"is_ajax":"1"
				}
				,success:function(response){
					callOnLoad
=
null;
					
					_gaq.push(['karnaval._trackPageview',
toOpen]);
					
					$('.ct').each(function(index,
element)
{
						var
code
=
$(element).data('codetabs');	
						if(typeof
code
!==
"undefined")
							code.destroy(true);
					});
					
					$(".main
>
.content_wrapper").html(response);
					$(window).scrollTop(0);
					
					try{
						if(response.indexOf("playbuzz")
>
0){
							if(typeof(PlayBuzz)
!==
"undefined")
								PlayBuzz.core.render();
						}	
					}
catch(exception){}

					
					try{
						window.instgrm.Embeds.process()
					}
catch(exception){}	
					
					
					if($(".main
>
.content_wrapper
#meta").length
>
0){
						$("body").attr("class",$(".main
>
.content_wrapper
#meta").attr("body_class"));
						$("head
title").text($(".main
>
.content_wrapper
#meta").attr("page_title"));
						
						$("meta[property='og:url']").attr("content",$(".main
>
.content_wrapper
#meta").attr("page_url"));
						$("meta[property='og:description']").attr("content",$(".main
>
.content_wrapper
#meta").attr("page_description"));
						$("meta[property='og:title']").attr("content",$(".main
>
.content_wrapper
#meta").attr("page_title"));
						$("meta[property='og:image']").attr("content",$(".main
>
.content_wrapper
#meta").attr("page_thumbnail"));
						
						$("link[rel='canonical']").attr("href",$(".main
>
.content_wrapper
#meta").attr("page_url"));
						try{
							if(typeof(VK._pData)
!==
"undefined"){
								VK._pData.title			=
$(".main
>
.content_wrapper
#meta").attr("page_title");
								VK._pData.image			=
$(".main
>
.content_wrapper
#meta").attr("page_thumbnail");
								VK._pData.url			=
$(".main
>
.content_wrapper
#meta").attr("page_url");
								VK._pData.description	=
$(".main
>
.content_wrapper
#meta").attr("page_description");
							}
						}
catch
(exception){
							debug("Trouble
updating
VK
data");
						}
					}
					else{
						if($("body").hasClass("branch-banner-is-active")){
							$("body").attr("class","branch-banner-is-active");
						}
						else{
							$("body").attr("class","");
						}
						$("head
title").text("Chameleon");
					}
					
					if(log_history){
						try{
							history.pushState({url:toOpen,is_local:true},"Test",toOpen);
						}
						catch(exception){
							debug('Exception
in
open
Page');
							debug(exception);
						}
						
					}
					if(typeof
callOnLoad
===
"function"){
						try{
							callOnLoad();
							if(typeof
addthis
!==
"undefined")
								addthis.layers.refresh();
						}
						catch(exception){
							debug('Exception
in
open
Page:
callonload');
							debug(exception);
						}
						
						
					}
					
					initializeBanners();
					loadImages();
				}
			});
		}
		function
setPlayerHeight(){
			var
scrollPos
=
$(window).scrollTop();
				
			var
superBarHeight
=
45;
			if($(".superbar
nav").hasClass("open"))
				superBarHeight
=
92;
				
			var
newHeight
=
superBarHeight
-
scrollPos;
			if(newHeight
<
0)
				newHeight
=
0;
			
			$(".superbar").addClass("on_scroll").height(newHeight);
			if(newHeight
==
superBarHeight)
				$(".superbar").removeClass("on_scroll");
			if($("body
>
.station_list_container").hasClass('open')){
				if($(window).width()
>
480){
					$(".station_list_container").css("top",$("header").height());
					$(".station_list_container
.station_list
.station_item:last-child").css("margin-bottom",$("header").height());
				}
			}
		}
		
		function
loadImages(){
			$(".main
.thumb_container
img:not(.loaded)").each(function(index,
img)
{
				if($(img).offset().top-$(window).height()+100
<
$(window).scrollTop()
&&
$(img).offset().top
>
$(window).scrollTop()
&&
!$(img).hasClass("loaded")){
					$(img).addClass("loaded").attr("src",$(img).attr("org_src"));
				}
			});
			
			$(".main
.banner_container.initialized:not(.loaded)").each(function(index,
banner_container)
{
				try{
					if($(banner_container).offset().top-$(window).height()+100
<
$(window).scrollTop()
||
$(banner_container).hasClass("pageskin")
||
$(banner_container).hasClass("full_size")
||
$(banner_container).hasClass("inread")
||
$(banner_container).hasClass("new_banner")
||
$(banner_container).hasClass("leaderboard")){
					$(banner_container).addClass("loaded");
					
					var
container_id
	=
$(".banner_wrapper
.banner",banner_container).attr("id");
					
					var
banner_width
=
0;
					var
banner_height
=
0;
					
					if($(banner_container).data("width")
!=
""
&&
$(banner_container).data("height")
!=
""){
						banner_width
	=
$(banner_container).data("width");
						banner_height
	=
$(banner_container).data("height");
					}
					
					var
banner_code
=
"https://a.adwolf.ru/prepareCode?pp=cl&ps=cek&p2=fu&pct=a&plp=a&pli=a&pop=a&pr=";
					if($(banner_container).data("banner_code")
!=
""){
						banner_code
=
$(banner_container).data("banner_code");
					}
					
					$(".banner_wrapper
.banner",banner_container).html("");
					
					var
extra_params
=
{};
					
					if($(banner_container).hasClass("pageskin")
||
$(banner_container).hasClass("full_size")
||
$(banner_container).hasClass("new_banner")
||
$(banner_container).hasClass("inread")){
						extra_params
=
{mechanics:2};
					}
					
					var
user_details
=
{};
					if(karnaval_member
!=
null){
						try{
							var
gender
=
(karnaval_member.gender
==
"F"
?
"f"
:
"m");
							var
dob
=
karnaval_member.dob;
							var
current_year
=
new
Date().getFullYear();
							var
age
=
"";
							
							dob_split
=
dob.split("-");
							
							if(dob_split.length
==
3){
								dob
=
parseInt(dob_split[0]);
								if(dob
>
0)
									age
=
current_year
-
dob;
							}
							
							user_details
=
	{
											

puid1:gender
											
,puid2:age
											
,uuid
:
karnaval_member.id
											}
						}
						catch(exception){
							user_details
=
{};
						}
					}
					active_banners[container_id]
	=
new
Adwolf({
															
placeholderId	:
container_id
															,width			:
banner_width
															,height			:
banner_height
															,link			:
banner_code
														
}
														,{puids:user_details}
														,{paps:{}}
														,extra_params
													);
					
					
				}
				}
catch
(e){}
			});
		}

		function
initializeBanners(){
			
			$(".main
.banner_container:not(.initialized)").each(function(index,

				catch(e){}
			});
			//googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
			loadImages();
		
		}
		
		
		function
initializeSmiNews(array){
			if($(".smi_unit").length
>
0){
				$.each(array,
function(index,
value)
{
				

(function()
{
					var
sc
=
document.createElement('script');
sc.type
=
'text/javascript';
sc.async
=
true;
					sc.src
=
'https://smi2.ru/data/js/'+value+'.js';
sc.charset
=
'utf-8';
					var
s
=
document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
s.parentNode.insertBefore(sc,
s);
				

}());
				

$("#unit_"+value).css("display","block");
				});
			}
		}
		
		function
selectRBCWidgetItem(to_select){
			var
item_selected
=
$(to_select).closest(".widget_item");
			var
parent
=
$(item_selected).closest(".rbc_content");
			var
type
=
$(item_selected).attr("type");
			var
id
=
$(item_selected).attr("widget_item_id");
			$("iframe",parent).attr("src","rbc_player.php?item_id="+id);
			$(".widget_item.active").removeClass("active");
			$(item_selected).addClass("active");
		}	
		
		/*REGAUTH*/
		function
toggleRegauthForm(to_show){
			$(".regauth_container:visible").slideUp(function(){
				$(".error_container",$(this)).hide();
				$(".error_container
ul",$(this)).html("");	
				$("."
+
to_show
+
"_container.regauth_container").slideDown();
			});
			checkCountry($("#country"));
		}
		function
popLogin(){
			checkCountry($("#country"));
			if($(".regauth_popup_container").is(":visible")){
				toggleRegauthForm("login");
			}
			else{
				$(".regauth_container").hide();
				$(".login_container.regauth_container").show();
				$(".regauth_popup_container").slideDown();
			}
		}
		function
popSignup(){
			checkCountry($("#country"));
			if($(".regauth_popup_container").is(":visible")){
				toggleRegauthForm("signup");
			}
			else{
				$(".regauth_container").hide();
				$(".signup_container.regauth_container").show();
				$(".regauth_popup_container").slideDown();
			}
		}
		function
closeRegauth(){
			$(".regauth_popup_container").slideUp();		
		}
		
		var
karnaval_member
=

		function
checkCountry(to_check){
			if($(to_check).val()
==
"RU"){
				$(".city_container
.select_container",$(to_check).closest(".form_container")).show();
				$(".city_container
input",$(to_check).closest(".form_container")).hide();
			}
			else{
				$(".city_container
.select_container",$(to_check).closest(".form_container")).hide();
				$(".city_container
input",$(to_check).closest(".form_container")).show();
			}
		}

		}
		function
updateMemberInfo(){
			closeRegauth();
			if(karnaval_member
!=
null){
				$(".member_area
a").html("Выйти").attr("onclick","logout();");	
				$(".member_area
.member_name").html("<a
href='profile.php'>"+((karnaval_member.first_name.length
>=
12)
?
(karnaval_member.first_name).substring(0,
10)+"..."
:
karnaval_member.first_name)

+
"
"
+
(karnaval_member.last_name).substring(0,1)
+
".</a>");
				$(".member_area
img").attr("src",karnaval_member.profile_image);
				$(".member_area
img").fadeIn();
			}
			else{
				$(".member_area
.member_name").html("<a
href='javascript:;'
onclick='popLogin()'>Войти</a>
");
				$(".member_area
>
a").attr("onclick","popSignup();").html("Зарегистрироваться");	
				$(".member_area
img").fadeOut(function(){
					$(".member_area
img").attr("src","");
				});
			}
			
			$(".member_area").fadeIn();
			initializeBanners();
		}
		function
getLoggedInMember(count){
			if(typeof
count
==
"undefined")
				count
=
0;
			
			$.ajax({
				url:
"/functions/member.functions.php",
				data:{
					"command"
:
"get_logged_in_member"
				},
				type:"POST",
				dataType:
'json',
				timeout:5000,
				success:
function
(response)
{
					if(response.result)
						karnaval_member
=
response.data;
					else
						karnaval_member
=
null;
						
					updateMemberInfo();
					closeRegauth();
				},
				error:
function(x,
t,
m)
{
					if(t==="timeout"
&&
count
<
5)
{
						karnaval_member
=
null;
						count++;
						updateLogin(count);
					}
else
{
						karnaval_member
=
null;
					}
				},
				complete:function(){	}
			});

		}
		function
logout(count){
			if(typeof
count
==
"undefined")
				count
=
0;
			
			$.ajax({
				url:
"/functions/member.functions.php",
				data:{
					"command"
:
"logout"
				},
				type:"POST",
				dataType:
'json',
				timeout:5000,
				success:
function
(response)
{
					if(response.result){
						karnaval_member
=
null;
						updateMemberInfo();	
						openLink("/");
					}
				},
				error:
function(x,
t,
m)
{
					if(t==="timeout"
&&
count
<
5)
{
						count++;
						logout(count);
					}

				},
				complete:function(){	}
			});

		}
		function
login(button_clicked,count){
			if(typeof
count
===
"undefined")
				count
=
0;
				
			if(typeof
button_clicked
===
"undefined"
||
$(button_clicked).length
==
0){
				return
false;
			}
			var
container
=
$(button_clicked).closest(".form_container");
			if(typeof
container
===
"undefined"
||
$(container).length
==
0){
				return
false;
			}
		
			var
form_values
=
getFormValues(container);
			if(!$.isEmptyObject(form_values.errors)){
				return
false
			}
			
			var
post_data
=
form_values.data;
			post_data.command
=
"login";
			
			$.ajax({
				
url
		:
"/functions/member.functions.php"
				,data
		:
post_data
				,type
		:
"POST"
				,dataType
	:
'json'
				,timeout		:
5000
				,success		:
function(response){
					if(response.result){
						karnaval_member
=
response.data;
						updateMemberInfo();
					}
else
{
						$(".error_container
ul",container).html("");
						var
messages
=
[];
						if(typeof
response.messages
!==
"undefined"){
							messages
=
response.messages;
						}
						if(messages.length
<
1)
							messages
=
["An
unidentified
error
has
occured.
Please
try
again
later!"];
							
						$.each(messages,function(index,message){
							if($.trim(message)
!=
"")
								$(".error_container
ul",container).append("<li>"+message+"</li>");
						});
						
						$(".error_container",container).slideDown();
					}
				}
				,error		:
function(x,
t,
m)
{
					if(t==="timeout"
&&
count
<
5)
{
						count++;
						login(button_clicked,count);
					}

				}
			});
		}
		function
recover(button_clicked,count){
			$(".error_container",container).slideUp();
			if(typeof
count
===
"undefined")
				count
=
0;
				
			if(typeof
button_clicked
===
"undefined"
||
$(button_clicked).length
==

		function
getFormValues(container){
			var
to_return
=
{"data":{},"errors":{}};
			$(".error",$(container)).removeClass("error");
			$(".field",$(container)).each(function(index,
element)
{
				var
key
		=
$(element).attr("key");
				
				if(key
!=
null
&&
key
!=
""){
					var
value
	=
$.trim($(element).val());
					
					if($(element).is(":radio")){
						var
name
=
$(element).attr("name");
						value
=
$('input[name='+name+']:checked',
container).val()

					}
					if($(element).is(":checkbox")){
						value
=
$(element).is(":checked")
?
"1"
:
"0";
					}
					
					if($(element).hasClass("forced")
&&
value
==
""){
						$(element).addClass("error");
						$(element).closest(".field_container").addClass("error");
						to_return.errors[key]
=
$(element).attr("error_message");
					}
					
					to_return.data[key]
=
value;
				}
			});
			
			return
to_return;
		}

		function

			$(".superbar").animate({height:92},200);
			$(".superbar

			$(".main").animate({"padding-top":"+=46"},200);
			$(".station_list_container").animate({"top":"163"},200);
		}
		function
closeNav(){
			$(".superbar").animate({height:46},200);
			$(".superbar
nav").removeClass("open");
			if($(window).width()
<
720)
				$(".superbar
nav").slideUp(200);
			else
				$(".superbar
nav").removeAttr("style");

				
			$(".main").animate({"padding-top":"-=46"},200);
			$(".station_list_container").animate({"top":"117"},200);
		}	
		function
toggleNav(){
			if($(".superbar
nav").hasClass("open"))
				closeNav();
			else
				openNav();
		}

		function
check_tabs(){
			debug("Checking
tabs");
			
			if(player_tab_check_timeout
!=
null)
				clearTimeout(player_tab_check_timeout);
				
			
			if(is_playing){
				try{
					if(localStorage.getItem("active_player_tab")
!=
random_tab_player_key){
						debug("Player
active
on
another
tab!
Calling
stop!",true);
						togglePlay();
					}
					player_tab_check_timeout
=
setTimeout(function(){check_tabs();},5000);
				}
catch(exception){
					debug("Localstorage
not
supported!",true);
					return
false;
				}	
			}
			
			player_tab_check_timeout
=
setTimeout(function(){check_tabs();},5000);
		}

					clearTimeout(player_tab_check_timeout);
			}

		function
updateCommentCount(){
			var
last_article
=
$(".main_article_wrapper
.article_scroll_container").last();
			
			if($(".vk_comment_count",last_article).html()
!=
"")
				return;
				
			VK.Api.call(
				'widgets.getComments',
				{
					
widget_api_id	:
"5039324"
					,url			:
last_article.data("article_url")
					,page_id		:
"article_"
+
last_article.data("article_id")
				},
				function(response){
					if(!$.isEmptyObject(response)
&&
!$.isEmptyObject(response.response)){
						if(!isNaN(response.response.count))
							$(".vk_comment_count",last_article).html(response.response.count);
					}
				}
			);
			
			setTimeout(function(){updateCommentCount();},5000);
		}

{

window
).resize(function()
{
				var
currentScroll
=

(($("body").width()

/

+

					if($(window).scrollTop()
>
fixmeTop
+

						$('.static_right_column').addClass('static_right_column_fixed').css({top:
$(window).height()-$('.static_right_column').height()
+'px'});

						$('.static_right_column').removeClass('static_right_column_fixed').css({right:
(($("body").width()
-
$(".main
>
.content_wrapper").width())
/

+
"px"});
					}
				}
			});

===
undefined)

		function
callOnLoad(){
			
			var
last_article
=
$(".main_article_wrapper
.article_scroll_container").last();
			
			$(".vk_comments",last_article).html("");		
			$(".vk_groups",last_article).html("");		

			updateCommentCount();
			initializeSmiNews(article_smi_array);
			/**/
			$('.static_right_column').css({right:
(($("body").width()
-
$(".main
>
.content_wrapper").width())
/
2)
+
"px"});
			
			/**/
			

			$(".kplayer_container",last_article).each(function(index,value){
				var
playerId
		=
$("div",$(value)).attr("id");
				var
videoURL
		=
$("div",$(value)).attr("kplayer_url");
				var
posterURL
		=
$("div",$(value)).attr("kplayer_thumbnail");
				var
videoTitle		=
$("div",$(value)).attr("kplayer_title");
				var
pWidth
			=
$(value).width();
				var
pHeight
			=
Math.floor(pWidth*9/16);
				var
autoPlay
		=
false;
				
				jwplayer(playerId).setup({
					file			:
videoURL,
					width			:
"100%",
					//height			:
pHeight,
					title			:
videoTitle,
					image			:
posterURL,
					displaytitle
	:
false,
					autostart
		:
autoPlay,
					androidhls		:
true,
					aspectratio		:
"16:9",
					skin			:
'bekle',
					abouttext		:
"Chameleon
FM",
					aboutlink		:
"https://chameleon.fm",
					advertising		:
null
				});
				
			});		
							if(typeof(YT)
!=
"undefined"){
					loadYTVideos();	
				}
						if(typeof(PlayBuzz)
!==
"undefined")
				PlayBuzz.core.render();
				
		}
		function
popGallery(toPop){
			
			var
popup_container
=
$("#gallery_popup_"+toPop);
			var
element
=
$('.gallery_container
.ct',popup_container);
			var
container
=
$(element).closest(".gallery_container");
			var
gallery
=
null;
			if(!$(container).hasClass("loaded")){		
				$("img",container).each(function(index,
image)
{
					$(image).attr("src",$(image).attr("org_src"));
				});
			}
			$(element).codetabs({
				fx
:
'line',
				speed
:
1200,
				isSlideshow
:
'true',
				isAutoRun
:'true',
				slideshow
:{
					isHoverPause:'true',
					delay
:
8000		
				},
				swipe
:
{
isBody
:
true
}
			});
			
			gallery
=
$(element).data('codetabs');
			
			gallery.ev.on('init',
function()
{
$(container).addClass("loaded");});

			
			gallery.ev.on('selectID',
function(e,
slide_id)
{
				var
active_slide
=
$(".gallery_container
.ct-slide",popup_container).get(slide_id);
				
				$(".gallery_description_container
.gallery_title",popup_container).html($("img",active_slide).data("title"));
				$(".gallery_description_container
.gallery_description",popup_container).html($("img",active_slide).data("description"));
				
				
				$(".counter_countainer
.current",container).html((slide_id+1));
			});

			$(".arrow_container.left",container).click(function(){
				gallery.prev();
			});
			$(".arrow_container.right",container).click(function(){
				gallery.next();
			});
			
			$(popup_container).slideDown();
			$(window).scrollTop(0);
				
		}
		
		function
closeGallery(){
			var
active_gallery
=
$(".gallery_popup_container:visible");
			$(active_gallery).slideUp(function(){
				var
element
=
$('.gallery_container
.ct',active_gallery);
				gallery
=
$(element).data('codetabs');
				gallery.destroy();
			});
		}
